vary in range, from extremely unpleasant to mind-blowing awesome. travel.</p>\n\t \t\t\t\t\t</div>\n\t\t\t\t\t</div><!--/mag-content-->\n\n                    <div class=\"mag-meta clearfix\">\n                    <span class=\"alignleft mag-date\">July 28,
